def get_vax_name(keyword):
    if 'pfizer' in keyword or 'pfs' in keyword:
        return 'COMIRNATY PFS (Pfizer-BioNTech)'
    elif'moderna' in keyword or'mRNA' in keyword:
        return 'COVID-19 mRNA Vaccine Moderna'
    else:
        return None

11205,"###Write down your answer here.

""""""

import json
from elasticsearch import Elasticsearch
es = Elasticsearch()


def get_data(index):
    res = es.search(
        index=index, 
        body={
            ""query"": {
                ""match"" : {""STATE"":""MO""}
            }
        },
        size=10000)

    return [x['_source'] for x in res['hits']['hits']]

def main():
    data = get_data('vaers-january-2021')
    print(""Number of records:"", len(data))
    #print(json.dumps(data[0], indent=4))

if __name__ == ""__main__"":
    main()"

import json

def get_es_client():
    es = None

    try:
        # Connect to local elasticsearch instance
        es = Elasticsearch(hosts=[{""host"": ""localhost"", ""port"": 9200}], timeout=300)

        if not es.ping():
            raise ConnectionError(""Elasticsearch service unavailable"")

    except Exception as e:
        print(e)
        sys.exit()

    return es

def get_vax_name(keyword):
    if 'tdap' in keyword or 'Tdap' in keyword:
        return '<NAME>'
    elif 'hep a' in keyword or 'Hep A' in keyword:
        return '<NAME>'
    else:
        print('No match')


def generate_es_query(field_name, keyword):
    es_query = {
        ""query"": {
            ""bool"": {
                ""must"": [
                    {
                        ""match"": {
                            f""{field_name}"": keyword
                        }
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }

    return es"

def get_keyword(question):
    #print(""Question:"", question)
    keywords = []
    for word in question.split():
        if word not in stopwords:
            keywords.append(word)

    return keywords


def extract_field_name(keywords):
    fields = {}
    for key in keywords:
        if key in FIELD_NAMES:
            fields[key] = FIELD_NAMES[key]
    
    return fields"

def get_keyword(question):
    # Extract the keyword from the question
    keyword = re.search('(?<=\s).*?(?=\s)', question)
    if not keyword:
        return None

    return keyword[0]

from elasticsearch import Elasticsearch
es = Elasticsearch()


# In[2]:


def search(index, body):
    res = es.search(index=index, body=body)
    return [r['_source'] for r in res['hits']['hits']]

def get_keyword(question):
    # Extract the keyword from the question
    keyword = re.search('(?<=\s).*?(?=\.)', question)

    if not keyword:
        return None
    
    return keyword[0]


def get_field_name(keyword):
    # Get the field name by matching the keyword to a list of keywords
    for key in KEYWORDS:
        if keyword == key['keyword']:
            return key['field']

    return None

    # Extract the keyword from the question
    keyword = re.search('###(.*)###', question).group(1)

    return keyword


def get_field_name(keyword):
    # Extract the field name from the keyword
    field_name = re.search('###Elasticsearch database with field names:(.*)###', keyword).group(1)
    
    # Remove the leading and trailing spaces in the field name
    field_name = field_name.strip()

    # Split the field name by comma
    field_names = field_name"

def get_keyword(question):
    # Extract the keyword from the question
    keyword = re.search('###(.*)###', question).group(1)

    return keyword


def get_field_name(keyword):
    # Extract the field name from the keyword
    field_name = re.search('###Elasticsearch database with field names:(.*)###', keyword).group(1)
    
    # Remove spaces in the field name
    field_name"

2564,"### What is the answer to the question?
### Generate the SQL query for this question.
""""""


def get_question(text):
    """"""
    Extracts the question from a text string.

    Args:
        text (str): The input text string.

    Returns:
        str: The extracted question or None if no question was found in the
            text.
    """"""
    # Split into sentences
    sentences = sent_tokenize(text)
    # Find first sentence containing '?'
    for i, s in enumerate(sentences):
        if ""?"" in s:
            return s[s.find(""?"") + 1 :]
    else:
        return None


def get_answer(text):
    """"""
    Extracts the answer from a text string.

    Args:
        text (str): The input text string.

    Returns:
        str: The extracted answer or None if no answer was found in the text.
    """"""
    # Split into sentences
    sentences ="

    """"""
    This function takes a natural language question as input and returns an elasticsearch query that can be used to retrieve relevant documents from the clinical notes index in elasticsearch.

    Parameters
    ----------
    question : str
        The natural language question to be answered by the system.

    Returns
    -------
    es_query : dict
        An elasticsearch query that can be used to retrieve relevant documents from the clinical notes index in elasticsearch.

    """"""
    
    # Extract keywords from the question using spaCy's nlp model.
    doc = nlp(question)
    keywords = [token.text for token in doc if not token.is_stop]
    
    # Get the first keyword which will be the main keyword of the question.
    keyword = keywords[0].lower()

2612,"### What is the answer to the question?
### Generate the SQL query for this question.
""""""


def get_question(text):
    """"""
    Extracts the question from a text string.

    Args:
        text (str): The input text string.

    Returns:
        str: The extracted question.
    """"""
    return re.search(""(?<=Prompt:\n).*?(?=Answer)"", text, flags=re.DOTALL)[
        0
    ].strip()


def get_answer(text):
    """"""
    Extracts the answer from a text string.

    Args:
        text (str): The input text string.

    Returns:
        str: The extracted answer.
    """"""
    return re.search(""(?<=Answer:\n).*?(?=Prompt|Clinical Notes)"", text, flags=re.DOTALL)[
        0
    ].strip()

    keyword = tokens[0].lower()
    print(""Keyword:"", keyword)

def get_question(text):
    """"""
    Extracts the question from a text string.

    Args:
        text (str): The input text string.

    Returns:
        str: The extracted question.
    """"""
    return re.search(""(?<=Prompt:\n).*?(?=Answer)"", text, flags=re.DOTALL)[
        0
    ].strip()


def get_answer(text):
    """"""
    Extracts the answer from a text string.

    Args:
        text (str): The input text string.

    Returns:
        str: The extracted answer.
    """"""
    return re.search(""(?<=Answer:\n).*?(?=Prompt|Clinical Notes)"", text, flags=re.DOTALL)[
        0
    ].strip()

###What is the field name?
###Generate the Elasticsearch query based on the filed name and keyword.
Clinical Notes: ###Give me all the patients whose age is less than or equal to 70. 
Answer:
{
    ""query"": {
        ""range"" : {
            ""AGE_YRS"" : {
                ""lte"":70
            }
        }
    }
}

### Generate the SQL query for this question.

### Execute the SQL query in MySQL Workbench.
Result: California, Tex"

""""""

def get_question(text):
    """"""
    Extracts the question from text

    Parameters
    ----------
    text : str
        Text containing the question

    Returns
    -------
    question : str
        Question extracted from text
    """"""
    return re.search('(?<=\n).*?(?=Prompt)', text).group()


def get_answer(text):
    """"""
    Extracts the answer from text

    Parameters
    ----------
    text : str
        Text containing the answer

    Returns
    -------
    answer : str
        Answer extracted from text
    """"""
    return re.search('(?<=\n).*?(?=Prompt|Question)', text).group().strip('\n')


def get_field_name(text):

def get_keyword(question):
    #print(""Question:"", question)
    keywords = []
    for word in question.split():
        if word[0] == '#':
            continue
        elif word[-1] == '?':
            keywords.append(word[:-1])
        else:
            keywords.append(word)

    return keywords


def extract_field_name(keywords):
    fields = []
    for keyword"

def search(index=""vaers"", body=None):
    """"""
    Search for documents in Elasticsearch index

    Parameters
    ----------
    index : str
        Name of the Elasticsearch index (default ""vaers"")
    body : dict or list
        Query body as either dictionary or JSON string

    Returns
    -------
    hits : generator
        Generator object yielding results from Elasticsearch query
    """"""
    if isinstance(body, dict):
        # Convert dictionary to JSON string
        body = json.dumps(body)
    elif not isinstance(body, str):
        raise TypeError(""Body must be provided as either dictionary or JSON string."")

    # Perform search
    res = es.search(index=index,"

def main():
    es = Elasticsearch()

    # Question 1
    print(""Question 1"")
    q1_query = {
        ""size"": 0,
        ""_source"": [""RECVDATE""],
        ""aggs"": {
            ""march"": {""terms"": {""field"": ""RECVDATE"", ""order"": {""_count"": ""desc""}, ""size"": 5}}
        },
    }
    res = es.search(index=""vaersdata"", body=q1_query)
    print(json.dumps(res[""aggregations""][""march""][""buckets""]))"

6922,"{
    ""query"": {
        ""match"": {
            ""SYMPTOM_TEXT"": ""inflammation""
        }
    }
}

###Find all the cases where the vaccine recipient died from COVID-19.
Answer:
{
    ""query"": {
        ""bool"": {
            ""must"": [
                {
                    ""term"": {
                        ""DIED"": true
                    }
                },
                {
                    ""term"": {
                        ""STATE"": ""VA""
                    }
                }
            ]
        }
    }
}

###Find all the cases where the vaccine recipient was hospitalized for COVID-19.
Answer:
{
    ""query"": {
        ""bool"": {
            ""must"": [
                {
                    ""term"": {
                        ""HOSPITAL"": true
                    }
                },
                {
                    ""term"": {
                        ""STATE"": ""VA""
                    }
                }
            ]
        }
    }
}"

# In[10]:


# What is the number of patients who died in hospital?
query = {
    ""size"": 0,
    ""_source"": [""DIED""],
    ""aggs"" : {
        ""died_in_hospital"" : {
            ""filter"" : {""term"" : {""DIED"":""Y""}},
            ""aggs"" : {
                ""total_died_in_hospital"" : {
                    ""sum"" : {""field"" : ""HOSPDAYS""}
                }
            }
        }
    }
}
res = es.search(index=""vaers-index"", body=query)
print(""Number of patients who died in hospital:"", res['aggregations']['died_in_hospital']['total_died_"

def get_keyword(question):
    # Extract the keyword from the question
    keyword = re.search('(?<=\s).+?(?=\s)', question)

    if not keyword:
        return None
    
    return keyword[0]


def get_field_name(keyword):
    # Get the field name by matching the keyword in the dictionary
    for key, value in fields.items():
        if keyword == key or keyword in value:
            return value
    
    return None


def generate_elasticsearch_query(field_name, keyword):
    # Generate the elasticsearch query based on the field name and keyword
    return {
        'query': {
           'match': {
                f'{field_name}': keyword
            }
        }
    }"

    ----------

    Returns
    -------
    es_query : dict
        Dictionary containing the elasticsearch query.
    '''
